NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL  NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Director  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

NOTICE
FORM No. 151
(As per Rule 315)
Members' Voluntary Winding up
Notice of appointment of Liquidator pursuant to Section 516
Name of company
:
Baskar Chit Funds Private Limited
Nature of Business
:
Chit Fund Business
Address of Registered Office
:
No. 2, Javuli Bazaar, Ambur (T.N.)-635 802.
Name and Address of Liquidator :
Deepak Rathi,
Practising Company Secretary,
Flat No. 1C, Block 4, Arihant Vaikunth Apartment,
Purasawalkam, Chennai-600 007.
Notice is hereby given that  the Company in its' Annual General Meeting of the members of Baskar Chit Funds Private
Limited held on Thursday, 25th of June 2009, at the registered office of the Company, at No. 2, Javuli Bazaar,
Ambur-635 802, at 10.00 a.m., has unanimously passed the following resolution to wind up the company voluntarily.
Resolved that pursuant to the provisions of Section 484(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956 and the other applicable
provisions, the consent of the Company be and is hereby given for the winding up of the Company.
Resolved further that Mr. Deepak Rathi, Practising Company Secretary of Chennai, be and is hereby appointed as the
Liquidator of the Company for the purpose of winding up on a remuneration of Rs. 10,000/- plus out of pocket expenses
at actuals.
Resolved further that Mr. Deepak Rathi, Company Secretary, the Liquidator be and is hereby empowered to exercise all
powers as provided in sub-clauses (i) to (iv) of sub-section 457 of the Companies Act, 1956.
Chennai,
D.S. DEVARAJAN,
30th June 2009.
Director.
PRINTED AND PUBLISHED BY THE DIRECTOR OF STATIONERY AND PRINTING, CHENNAI
ON BEHALF OF THE GOVERNMENT OF TAMIL NADU
